### 3. [MobileFineTuner: A Unified End-to-End Framework for Fine-Tuning LLMs on Mobile Phones](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.08211)

**Authors**: Jiaxiang Geng, Lunyu Zhao, Yiyi Lu, Bing Luo  
**Category**: cs.LG  
**Published**: 2025-12-10  
**Score**: 9.5  
**Type**: new  
**ArXiv ID**: 2512.08211v1  

#### Abstract
Mobile phones are the most ubiquitous end devices, generating vast amounts of human-authored data and serving as the primary platform for end-side applications. As high-quality public data for large language models (LLMs) approaches exhaustion, on-device fine-tuning provides an opportunity to levera...

## 1. è®ºæ–‡çš„ä¸»è¦è´¡çŒ®å’Œåˆ›æ–°ç‚¹

### è§£å†³çš„é—®é¢˜
å½“å‰å¤§å‹è¯­è¨€æ¨¡å‹ï¼ˆLLMsï¼‰ä¾èµ–é«˜è´¨é‡å…¬å…±æ•°æ®è¿›è¡Œè®­ç»ƒï¼Œä½†ç ”ç©¶è¡¨æ˜è¿™ç±»æ•°æ®å¯èƒ½åœ¨2026â€“2032å¹´é—´è€—å°½ã€‚ä¸æ­¤åŒæ—¶ï¼Œæµ·é‡ç§æœ‰ç”¨æˆ·æ•°æ®å­˜å‚¨åœ¨ç»ˆç«¯è®¾å¤‡ï¼ˆå°¤å…¶æ˜¯ç§»åŠ¨æ‰‹æœºï¼‰ä¸Šï¼Œå…·æœ‰é«˜åº¦ä¸ªæ€§åŒ–ä»·å€¼ã€‚ç„¶è€Œï¼Œå°†è¿™äº›æ•æ„Ÿæ•°æ®ä¸Šä¼ è‡³æœåŠ¡å™¨è¿›è¡Œ fine-tuning å­˜åœ¨ä¸¥é‡çš„éšç§é£é™©ï¼ˆå¦‚è¿å GDPRï¼‰ï¼Œä¸”ç°æœ‰æ¡†æ¶å¤§å¤šä¸æ”¯æŒåœ¨çœŸå®ç§»åŠ¨è®¾å¤‡ä¸Šç›´æ¥å®Œæˆç«¯åˆ°ç«¯çš„ LLM fine-tuningã€‚

æ­¤å¤–ï¼Œä¸»æµ LLM æ¡†æ¶ï¼ˆå¦‚ PyTorchã€Hugging Face Transformersï¼‰åŸºäº Python æ„å»ºï¼Œè€Œç§»åŠ¨æ“ä½œç³»ç»Ÿï¼ˆå¦‚ Androidï¼‰å¹¶ä¸åŸç”Ÿæ”¯æŒ Pythonï¼Œå¯¼è‡´æ— æ³•ç›´æ¥éƒ¨ç½²ã€‚å·²æœ‰å°è¯•ï¼ˆå¦‚ PocketLLM å’Œ XPerTï¼‰å­˜åœ¨æ•ˆç‡ä½ã€å¼€å‘æˆæœ¬é«˜æˆ–ç¼ºä¹ç»Ÿä¸€å¼€æºæ¡†æ¶ç­‰é—®é¢˜ã€‚

### 4. [Prismatic World Model: Learning Compositional Dynamics for Planning in Hybrid Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.08411)

**Authors**: Mingwei Li, Xiaoyuan Zhang, Chengwei Yang, Zilong Zheng, Yaodong Yang  
**Category**: cs.AI  
**Published**: 2025-12-10  
**Score**: 9.0  
**Type**: new  
**ArXiv ID**: 2512.08411v1  

#### Abstract
Model-based planning in robotic domains is fundamentally challenged by the hybrid nature of physical dynamics, where continuous motion is punctuated by discrete events such as contacts and impacts. Conventional latent world models typically employ monolithic neural networks that enforce global conti...

### 5. [From Accuracy to Impact: The Impact-Driven AI Framework (IDAIF) for Aligning Engineering Architecture with Theory of Change](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.08449)

**Authors**: Yong-Woon Kim  
**Category**: cs.AI  
**Published**: 2025-12-10  
**Score**: 9.0  
**Type**: new  
**ArXiv ID**: 2512.08449v1  

#### Abstract
This paper introduces the Impact-Driven AI Framework (IDAIF), a novel architectural methodology that integrates Theory of Change (ToC) principles with modern artificial intelligence system design. As AI systems increasingly influence high-stakes domains including healthcare, finance, and public poli...

### 6. [Magneton: Optimizing Energy Efficiency of ML Systems via Differential Energy Debugging](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.08365)

**Authors**: Yi Pan, Wenbo Qian, Dedong Xie, Ruiyan Hu, Yigong Hu, Baris Kasikci  
**Category**: cs.DC  
**Published**: 2025-12-10  
**Score**: 9.0  
**Type**: new  
**ArXiv ID**: 2512.08365v1  

#### Abstract
The training and deployment of machine learning (ML) models have become extremely energy-intensive. While existing optimization efforts focus primarily on hardware energy efficiency, a significant but overlooked source of inefficiency is software energy waste caused by poor software design. This oft...

### 7. [Robust Agents in Open-Ended Worlds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.08139)

**Authors**: Mikayel Samvelyan  
**Category**: cs.LG  
**Published**: 2025-12-10  
**Score**: 8.5  
**Type**: new  
**ArXiv ID**: 2512.08139v1  

#### Abstract
The growing prevalence of artificial intelligence (AI) in various applications underscores the need for agents that can successfully navigate and adapt to an ever-changing, open-ended world. A key challenge is ensuring these AI agents are robust, excelling not only in familiar settings observed duri...

### 8. [An Agentic AI System for Multi-Framework Communication Coding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.08659)

**Authors**: Bohao Yang, Rui Yang, Joshua M. Biro, Haoyuan Wang, Jessica L. Handley, Brianna Richardson, Sophia Bessias, Nicoleta Economou-Zavlanos, Armando D. Bedoya, Monica Agrawal, Michael M. Zavlanos, Anand Chowdhury, Raj M. Ratwani, Kai Sun, Kathryn I. Pollak, Michael J. Pencina, Chuan Hong  
**Category**: cs.CL  
**Published**: 2025-12-10  
**Score**: 8.0  
**Type**: new  
**ArXiv ID**: 2512.08659v1  

#### Abstract
Clinical communication is central to patient outcomes, yet large-scale human annotation of patient-provider conversation remains labor-intensive, inconsistent, and difficult to scale. Existing approaches based on large language models typically rely on single-task models that lack adaptability, inte...

### 9. [Exposing Hidden Biases in Text-to-Image Models via Automated Prompt Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.08724)

**Authors**: Manos Plitsis, Giorgos Bouritsas, Vassilis Katsouros, Yannis Panagakis  
**Category**: cs.LG  
**Published**: 2025-12-10  
**Score**: 8.0  
**Type**: new  
**ArXiv ID**: 2512.08724v1  

#### Abstract
Text-to-image (TTI) diffusion models have achieved remarkable visual quality, yet they have been repeatedly shown to exhibit social biases across sensitive attributes such as gender, race and age. To mitigate these biases, existing approaches frequently depend on curated prompt datasets - either man...

# Exposing Hidden Biases in Text-to-Image Models via Automated Prompt Search è®ºæ–‡æ€»ç»“

## 1. è®ºæ–‡çš„ä¸»è¦è´¡çŒ®å’Œåˆ›æ–°ç‚¹

### è§£å†³çš„é—®é¢˜
å½“å‰æ–‡æœ¬åˆ°å›¾åƒï¼ˆText-to-Image, TTIï¼‰æ‰©æ•£æ¨¡å‹ï¼ˆå¦‚ Stable Diffusionã€DALLÂ·Eï¼‰åœ¨ç”Ÿæˆå›¾åƒæ—¶è¡¨ç°å‡ºæ˜¾è‘—çš„ç¤¾ä¼šåè§ï¼ˆsocial biasesï¼‰ï¼Œå°¤å…¶ä½“ç°åœ¨æ€§åˆ«ã€ç§æ—ã€å¹´é¾„ç­‰æ•æ„Ÿå±æ€§ä¸Šã€‚å°½ç®¡å·²æœ‰å¤šç§**å»åç½®ï¼ˆdebiasingï¼‰æ–¹æ³•**è¢«æå‡ºï¼Œä½†è¿™äº›æ–¹æ³•é€šå¸¸ä¾èµ–äºäººå·¥æ„å»ºæˆ–å¤§è¯­è¨€æ¨¡å‹ï¼ˆLLMï¼‰ç”Ÿæˆçš„**å›ºå®šæç¤ºè¯æ•°æ®é›†ï¼ˆcurated prompt datasetsï¼‰**è¿›è¡Œè®­ç»ƒæˆ–è¯„ä¼°ã€‚

è¿™ç§åšæ³•å­˜åœ¨ä¸¤ä¸ªæ ¸å¿ƒé—®é¢˜ï¼š
- **è¦†ç›–ä¸è¶³ï¼ˆCoverage Problemï¼‰**ï¼šä»…æµ‹è¯•æœ‰é™çš„æç¤ºç©ºé—´ï¼Œå¯èƒ½é—æ¼æœªé¢„è§çš„ã€è¯­å¢ƒè§¦å‘çš„éšæ€§åè§ã€‚
- **å¯è§£é‡Šæ€§å·®**ï¼šåŸºäºæ¢¯åº¦ä¼˜åŒ–çš„æ–¹æ³•è™½èƒ½å‘ç°é«˜åè§åŒºåŸŸï¼Œä½†ç”Ÿæˆçš„æç¤ºä¸å¯è¯»ï¼ˆå¦‚ `"nurse kerala matplotlib tbody"`ï¼‰ï¼Œéš¾ä»¥ç”¨äºå®é™…å®¡è®¡æˆ–ç†è§£åè§æœºåˆ¶ã€‚

### æå‡ºçš„æ–°æ–¹æ³•ï¼šBias-Guided Prompt Search (BGPS)
æœ¬æ–‡æå‡ºäº† **Bias-Guided Prompt Search (BGPS)**ï¼Œä¸€ç§**è‡ªåŠ¨æœç´¢å¯è§£é‡Šæç¤ºè¯ä»¥æœ€å¤§åŒ–æš´éœ² TTI æ¨¡å‹ä¸­éšè—åè§**çš„æ¡†æ¶ã€‚

#### æ–¹æ³•æ ¸å¿ƒæ€æƒ³
BGPS ç»“åˆäº†ä»¥ä¸‹ä¸¤ç§æŠ€æœ¯ï¼š
1. **Large Language Model (LLM)**ï¼šä½œä¸ºâ€œè¯­è¨€å…ˆéªŒâ€ï¼Œç”Ÿæˆè¯­æ³•è‡ªç„¶ã€è¯­ä¹‰åˆç†çš„æç¤ºè¯ã€‚
2. **Attribute Classifiers**ï¼šè½»é‡çº§åˆ†ç±»å™¨ï¼Œä½œç”¨äºæ‰©æ•£æ¨¡å‹ä¸­é—´å±‚è¡¨ç¤ºï¼ˆUNet activationsï¼‰ï¼Œå®æ—¶è¯„ä¼°ç”Ÿæˆå›¾åƒä¸­çš„åè§ç¨‹åº¦ï¼ˆå¦‚æ€§åˆ«æ¯”ä¾‹ï¼‰ã€‚

é€šè¿‡å°†è¿™ä¸¤ä¸ªä¿¡å·ç»“åˆä¸ºä¸€ä¸ªè”åˆç›®æ ‡å‡½æ•°ï¼Œåœ¨è§£ç è¿‡ç¨‹ä¸­å¼•å¯¼ LLM å‘â€œé«˜åè§â€æ–¹å‘ç”Ÿæˆæç¤ºï¼Œä»è€Œå®ç°ï¼š
- é«˜æ•ˆæ¢ç´¢å¹¿é˜”çš„æç¤ºç©ºé—´ï¼›
- ä¿æŒè¾“å‡ºæç¤ºçš„**äººç±»å¯è¯»æ€§å’Œç°å®å¯ç”¨æ€§**ã€‚

#### æ•°å­¦å½¢å¼åŒ–ç›®æ ‡
$$
\max_s \underbrace{\log P(s)}_{\text{Language Prior}} + \lambda \cdot \underbrace{\frac{1}{K}\sum_{i=1}^K \log P(A=a|\mathbf{x}_0,\dots,\mathbf{e}_T,s)}_{\text{Bias Score from Classifier}}
$$
å…¶ä¸­ $P(s)$ æ¥è‡ª LLMï¼Œ$P(A=a|\cdot)$ æ¥è‡ªé¢„è®­ç»ƒçš„ attribute classifierã€‚

> âœ… **åˆ›æ–°ç‚¹æ€»ç»“**ï¼šé¦–æ¬¡å°† LLM çš„è¯­ä¹‰ç”Ÿæˆèƒ½åŠ›ä¸æ‰©æ•£æ¨¡å‹å†…éƒ¨è¡¨ç¤ºåˆ†æç›¸ç»“åˆï¼Œç”¨äºç³»ç»Ÿæ€§åœ°â€œçº¢é˜Ÿæµ‹è¯•â€ï¼ˆred-teamï¼‰TTI æ¨¡å‹ä¸­çš„ç¤¾ä¼šåè§ï¼Œå¡«è¡¥äº†è¦†ç›–ç‡ä¸å¯è§£é‡Šæ€§ä¹‹é—´çš„é¸¿æ²Ÿã€‚

### 10. [Neural Ordinary Differential Equations for Simulating Metabolic Pathway Dynamics from Time-Series Multiomics Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.08732)

**Authors**: Udesh Habaraduwa, Andrei Lixandru  
**Category**: cs.LG  
**Published**: 2025-12-10  
**Score**: 8.0  
**Type**: new  
**ArXiv ID**: 2512.08732v1  

#### Abstract
The advancement of human healthspan and bioengineering relies heavily on predicting the behavior of complex biological systems. While high-throughput multiomics data is becoming increasingly abundant, converting this data into actionable predictive models remains a bottleneck. High-capacity, datadri...

### 11. [SkipKV: Selective Skipping of KV Generation and Storage for Efficient Inference with Large Reasoning Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.07993)

**Authors**: Jiayi Tian, Seyedarmin Azizi, Yequan Zhao, Erfan Baghaei Potraghloo, Sean McPherson, Sharath Nittur Sridhar, Zhengyang Wang, Zheng Zhang, Massoud Pedram, Souvik Kundu  
**Category**: cs.AI  
**Published**: 2025-12-10  
**Score**: 7.5  
**Type**: new  
**ArXiv ID**: 2512.07993v1  

#### Abstract
Large reasoning models (LRMs) often cost significant key-value (KV) cache overhead, due to their linear growth with the verbose chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning process. This costs both memory and throughput bottleneck limiting their efficient deployment. Towards reducing KV cache size during infere...

## 1. è®ºæ–‡çš„ä¸»è¦è´¡çŒ®å’Œåˆ›æ–°ç‚¹

### è§£å†³çš„é—®é¢˜
å¤§å‹æ¨ç†æ¨¡å‹ï¼ˆLarge Reasoning Models, LRMsï¼‰åœ¨æ‰§è¡Œå¤æ‚æ¨ç†ä»»åŠ¡ï¼ˆå¦‚æ•°å­¦æ¨å¯¼ã€ä»£ç ç”Ÿæˆï¼‰æ—¶ï¼Œé€šå¸¸ä¾èµ–å†—é•¿çš„ **Chain-of-Thought (CoT)** æ¨ç†è¿‡ç¨‹ã€‚è¿™ä¸€è¿‡ç¨‹å¯¼è‡´ **Key-Value (KV) cache å†…å­˜å¼€é”€å·¨å¤§**ï¼Œä¸”éšæ¨ç†é•¿åº¦çº¿æ€§å¢é•¿ï¼Œé€ æˆä»¥ä¸‹ç“¶é¢ˆï¼š
- **å†…å­˜å‹åŠ›å¤§**ï¼šKV cache å¯èƒ½è¿œè¶…æ¨¡å‹å‚æ•°æœ¬èº«ï¼›
- **ååé‡å—é™**ï¼šè§£ç é˜¶æ®µå—å†…å­˜å¸¦å®½é™åˆ¶ï¼›
- **ç”Ÿæˆé•¿åº¦å¢åŠ **ï¼šç°æœ‰ KV å‹ç¼©æ–¹æ³•å› è¯­ä¹‰ä¸è¿è´¯åˆ é™¤ tokenï¼Œå¼•å‘æ¨¡å‹â€œè¿‡åº¦æ€è€ƒâ€ï¼ˆoverthinkingï¼‰ï¼Œé‡å¤éªŒè¯ç­”æ¡ˆï¼Œåè€Œå»¶é•¿è¾“å‡ºã€‚

æ­¤å¤–ï¼Œç°æœ‰æ–¹æ³•åœ¨ **multi-batch æ¨ç†åœºæ™¯ä¸‹å‡†ç¡®ç‡æ˜¾è‘—ä¸‹é™**ï¼Œä¸»å› æ˜¯å¡«å…… tokenï¼ˆpadding tokensï¼‰æµªè´¹äº†æœ‰é™çš„ KV é¢„ç®—ã€‚

---

### æå‡ºçš„æ–°æ–¹æ³•ï¼šSkipKV
SkipKV æ˜¯ä¸€ç§æ— éœ€è®­ç»ƒçš„ KV å‹ç¼©æ¡†æ¶ï¼Œé€šè¿‡åœ¨**å¥å­çº§åˆ«**è¿›è¡Œé€‰æ‹©æ€§è·³è¿‡ï¼ˆskippingï¼‰æ¥æå‡æ¨ç†æ•ˆç‡ã€‚å…¶æ ¸å¿ƒåˆ›æ–°åŒ…æ‹¬ï¼š

#### ï¼ˆ1ï¼‰**å¥å­çº§ KV å­˜å‚¨è·³è¿‡ï¼ˆSentence-level KV Storage Skippingï¼‰**
- å¼•å…¥ **Pairwise Sentence Similarity (PSS)** åº¦é‡ï¼ŒåŸºäºæœ€åä¸€å±‚éšè—çŠ¶æ€è®¡ç®—å¥å­ç›¸ä¼¼åº¦ï¼›
- å®šä¹‰â€œå†—ä½™å¥å¯¹â€ï¼ˆPSS â‰¥ 0.95ï¼‰ï¼Œä¼˜å…ˆç§»é™¤è¾ƒæ—©å‡ºç°çš„é«˜ç›¸ä¼¼å¥å­ï¼›
- è®¾è®¡ **cumulative scoring æœºåˆ¶**ï¼Œç»¼åˆè€ƒè™‘ token é‡è¦æ€§ã€å†—ä½™æ€§å’Œå¥å­ç›¸ä¼¼æ€§ï¼Œç¡®ä¿å…ˆåˆ å¥å†åˆ è¯ï¼›
- æå‡º **KV cache èŒƒå›´ç›‘æ§é€»è¾‘**ï¼ŒåŠ¨æ€ç»´æŠ¤ç”Ÿæˆç©ºé—´ä¸ç¼“å­˜ç©ºé—´ä¹‹é—´çš„å¥å­æ˜ å°„å…³ç³»ï¼Œä¿è¯ä¸€è‡´æ€§ã€‚

#### ï¼ˆ2ï¼‰**è‡ªé€‚åº” KV ç”Ÿæˆè·³è¿‡ï¼ˆAdaptive KV Generation Skippingï¼‰**

### 12. [Towards a Science of Scaling Agent Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.08296)

**Authors**: Yubin Kim, Ken Gu, Chanwoo Park, Chunjong Park, Samuel Schmidgall, A. Ali Heydari, Yao Yan, Zhihan Zhang, Yuchen Zhuang, Mark Malhotra, Paul Pu Liang, Hae Won Park, Yuzhe Yang, Xuhai Xu, Yilun Du, Shwetak Patel, Tim Althoff, Daniel McDuff, Xin Liu  
**Category**: cs.AI  
**Published**: 2025-12-10  
**Score**: 7.5  
**Type**: new  
**ArXiv ID**: 2512.08296v1  

#### Abstract
Agents, language model (LM)-based systems that are capable of reasoning, planning, and acting are becoming the dominant paradigm for real-world AI applications. Despite this widespread adoption, the principles that determine their performance remain underexplored, leaving practitioners to rely on he...

### ç›¸æ¯”ç°æœ‰æ–¹æ³•çš„ä¼˜åŠ¿

### 13. [The SMART+ Framework for AI Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.08592)

**Authors**: Laxmiraju Kandikatla, Branislav Radeljic

#### Abstract
Artificial Intelligence (AI) systems are now an integral part of multiple industries. In clinical research, AI supports automated adverse event detection in clinical trials, patient eligibility screening for protocol enrollment, and data quality validation. å…·ä½“é—®é¢˜åŒ…æ‹¬ï¼š

è¯¥æ¡†æ¶å°†ä¸Šè¿°ä¹é¡¹åŸåˆ™æ˜ å°„åˆ°AIç³»ç»Ÿçš„å®Œæ•´ç”Ÿå‘½å‘¨æœŸï¼ˆObjective Setting â†’ Requirements â†’ Design â†’ Verification â†’ Deployment â†’ Operation & Maintenanceï¼‰ï¼Œå¹¶ç»“åˆ**é£é™©åˆ†çº§æœºåˆ¶**ï¼ˆHigh/Medium/Low Riskï¼‰ï¼Œå®ç°æŒ‰éœ€é…ç½®æ²»ç†å¼ºåº¦ã€‚

### ç›¸æ¯”ç°æœ‰æ–¹æ³•çš„ä¼˜åŠ¿
| ç‰¹æ€§ | SMART+ Framework | ç°æœ‰æ¡†æ¶ï¼ˆå¦‚NISTã€OECDã€EUï¼‰ |
|------|------------------|-------------------------------|
| **å¯æ“ä½œæ€§** | âœ… æ˜ç¡®å„é˜¶æ®µæ£€æŸ¥ç‚¹ä¸è´£ä»»ä¸»ä½“ï¼ˆå¦‚RACIçŸ©é˜µï¼‰ | âŒ å¤šä¸ºåŸåˆ™æ€§å£°æ˜ï¼Œç¼ºå°‘æ‰§è¡Œç»†èŠ‚ |

### 14. [Unveiling Latent Knowledge in Chemistry Language Models through Sparse Autoencoders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.08077)

**Authors**: Jaron Cohen, Alexander G. Hasson, Sara Tanovic  
**Category**: cs.LG  
**Published**: 2025-12-10  
**Score**: 7.5  
**Type**: new  
**ArXiv ID**: 2512.08077v1  

#### Abstract
Since the advent of machine learning, interpretability has remained a persistent challenge, becoming increasingly urgent as generative models support high-stakes applications in drug and material discovery. Recent advances in large language model (LLM) architectures have yielded chemistry language m...

### 15. [gHAWK: Local and Global Structure Encoding for Scalable Training of Graph Neural Networks on Knowledge Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.08274)

**Authors**: Humera Sabir, Fatima Farooq, Ashraf Aboulnaga  
**Category**: cs.LG  
**Published**: 2025-12-10  
**Score**: 7.5  
**Type**: new  
**ArXiv ID**: 2512.08274v1  

#### Abstract
Knowledge Graphs (KGs) are a rich source of structured, heterogeneous data, powering a wide range of applications. A common approach to leverage this data is to train a graph neural network (GNN) on the KG. However, existing message-passing GNNs struggle to scale to large KGs because they rely on th...

## ğŸ“… Schedule

## ğŸš€ How to Use

1. **Fork this repository** to your GitHub account
2. **Customize the configuration** by editing `config.json`:
   - Add/remove arXiv categories (e.g., `cs.AI`, `cs.LG`, `cs.CL`)
   - Modify keywords to match your research interests
   - Adjust `max_papers` and `days_back` settings
3. **Enable GitHub Actions** in your repository settings
4. **The bot will automatically run daily** and update the README.md

## ğŸ“ Customization

### arXiv Categories
Common categories include:
- `cs.AI` - Artificial Intelligence
- `cs.LG` - Machine Learning
- `cs.CL` - Computation and Language
- `cs.CV` - Computer Vision
- `cs.NE` - Neural and Evolutionary Computing
- `stat.ML` - Machine Learning (Statistics)

### Keywords
Add keywords that match your research interests. The bot will search for these terms in paper titles and abstracts.

### Exclude Keywords
Add terms to exclude certain types of papers (e.g., "survey", "review", "tutorial").

## ğŸ” Manual Trigger

You can manually trigger the bot by:
1. Going to the "Actions" tab in your repository
2. Selecting "arXiv Bot Daily Update"
3. Clicking "Run workflow"
